set my_period [expr 1000 / $my_clk_freq_MHz]
5
set find_clock [ find port [list $my_clock_pin] ]
{clk}
if {  $find_clock != [list] } {
   set clk_name $my_clock_pin
   create_clock -period $my_period $clk_name
} else {
   set clk_name vclk
   create_clock -period $my_period -name $clk_name
}
